<P>jay1atu dadhibAmana prasanne rudra debatA

<P>maGgaLa bighnarAja bhUta bhabiSya gyAMtA | 1 |

<P>maGgaLa sadAnanda deba lambodara

<P>sapata sindhu gopyagalA yAhAra udara | 2 |

<P>maGgaLa paramabrahma sarUpa bINAy1eka

<P>pAza aMkuza gajabadana aTa triy1ambaka | 3 |

<P>meru tattulya yAhAra kin~chita beniAkhi

<P>abaniLe chAhiMle tu ye koTi brahmANDa dekhi | 4 |

<P>Dibi Dibi bajAi yAhAra DAki Dambharu

<P>hrude paitA yAhAra ananta nAga pheru | 5 |

<P>swAmI tripura badhagalA yAhAra buddhi baLe

<P>binay1e anubrate nAtha muM tumbhara pAdataLe | 6 |

<P>lAGgaTa bhrUGgaTa ye bikaTa batranATe

<P>mahAbharaha tANDaba AropaNa saMkoTe | 7 |

<P>zrI bighnarAja zrIcaraNa kamaLe

<P>mama citta bhaji ho tahiM rahu ye bhrasaLe | 8 |

[MBO-06-2]

<P>byAsaMkara srijane deba prasanna bighnarAja

<P>karaNa hoi lekhana kaluTi aizuryya | 9 |

<P>y1e saMsAra madhye muhiM se dekhili sarUpa

<P>tuhi se harantA deba kaLikALa darpa | 10 |

<P>kaLiyuga ban~chantA nAtha prasanne paramayogI

<P>dinakara bibAdeNa tu kALadarpa bhAn~ji | 11 |

<P>saday1e nArAy1aNa tu prasanne rudrakAzI

<P>zUdramuni sAroLa dAsa talay1e abhyAsi | 12 |

<H>{@pANDabaGka indraprasthe prabeza, dhrutarASTra san~jay1a saMbAda
<>o dhaumya purohitaGkara dUtapaNe
<>hastinA gamana@}

<P>zuNa ho caitana zrI mahAbhAratha udiyoga paboGg kathA

<P>yAhA hetu karipArile sabhAy1e hoiba bakatA | 1 |

<P>yebaNa grantha zuNile adhArmikahiM hoy1e bhigyaM

<P>yAha zuNileTi prANI huanti sarbagyaM | 2 |

<P>udiyoga paboGg kathA hrudagate lay1e kale

<P>zAhAsraku jitA hoi y1ehA unyeSi pArile | 3 |

<P>udiyoga paRhile druza hoai buddhi

<P>udiyoga paRhile prApata hoai ruddhi siddhi | 4 |

<P>udiyoga boliNa yebaNa grantha paboGg

<P>dharma artha kAma mokSa prApata y1ethuM sarba | 5 |

<P>caubarga sampada ye prApata brahmagyAna

<P>ASya dhana santAna hoiba barddhamAna | 6 |

<P>yAhA se srijanA kaleka agasti

<P>muhiM tAhA ban~chAili bicitra zuddha pothi | 7 |

[MBO-06-3]

<P>udiyoga paboGg zunimA nare bANI

<P>subuddhi paNDita sugyaM hoiba y1ehA zuNi | 8 |

<P>baibasuta manu pucchAkale agasti

<P>y1ethu anantare hoilA yisa rIti | 9 |

<P>zubhayoge pANDabe bAhAra matsyadezuM

<P>AkAze maGgaLa dhuni zubhai pANDabaMkara AsuM | 10 |

<P>birATa AgiANi samadaNDa gheni

<P>pacheNa pan~chALa kumAranta gheni zrIkhaNDI bhrAtha beni | 11 |

<P>zrIkruSNA dropatI ye koLa sambhASaNe

<P>pAn~chALIki prabodhile bahuta sanamAne | 12 |

<P>gopALI nadIkULe birATa prabodhi

<P>aneka binoy1I hoile birATa yathAbidhi | 13 |

<P>yujheSThi debe ye prabodhi bacana prakAzi

<P>bAhuDa birATa tu parama kalyANa hoasi | 14 |

<P>birATa praNapatya ye yujheSThiMka padmapAy1e

<P>muhiM yAiM kinA swAmI indraprazasta yAy1e | 15 |

<P>yujheSThi boile ho daNDa ghenigale

<P>mAnagobinda kopa karibanA parathATha dekhile | 16 |

<P>sahodraMka nimante kALaka bulili ghora bane

<P>Abara kimpe dharma laMghibi aLapa ye dine | 17 |

<P>zAnti samArjane Ambhe na karibA kaLi

<P>aSTa abadhAne ye zatruku sambhALi | 18 |

<P>birATa zrIkhaNDi ye bAhuDile sanya gheni

<P>tahuM se pANDabe caLile dibasa rajanI | 19 |

<P>pan~chatiriza dibase prabeza indraprazaste

<P>nagra bhitare yAi rahile pan~chu bhrAthe | 20 |

<P1>12|2--zAnti bhaji rahibA bahuta sanamAne | (ja, da, Na, ka, ba)

<P1>18|2--aSTa abadhAne zatruku saMghAri | (Ta, gha)

[MBO-06-4]

<P>bhAmasena boilA deba yibAnA AstAnaku

<P>dekhibA nAhi ki driyothana dhuzAsana bhISma droNa karNNaMku | 21 |

<P>yujheSThi debe boile jANimA tadanta

<P>bAratA pAi mAnagobinda niai kinA Ambhanta | 22 |

<P>ratha gaja azwa pAdAnti achanti saGge kete | 26 |

<P>Dagara patibAkya deba sAbadhAna bhabatu

<P>birATa daNDa gheni bAhuDi galA dharmapathuM | 27 |

<P>pANDaba pAn~chajaNa kumAra abhimanyu

<P>pAn~chALa kumAra tule bALuta ye tanu | 28 |

<P>y1eteka tule dekhilu Ana nAhiM aguLi | 29 |

<P>san~jay1e kahile dhrutarASTaMka Agare

<P>pANDabe prabeza hoile indraprazasta nabare | 30 |

<P>dhrutarASTa boile ho karibA kemanta

<P>bho daiba puruSa mote hoibA upagata | 31 |

<P>driyodhana kaNThe bijekaru kinA saraswatI

<P>pANDabe kaurabe yehne hoanti pIrati | 32 |

<P>san~jay1e boile rAjA na kara biLApa

<P>dharma abazeSe Asi barddhuta hoilA ki prApa | 33 |

[MBO-06-5]

<P>yujheSThi hrudagate nAhiMnA anIti

<P>sarbe manda aTanti nA tohora santati | 34 |

<P>yujheSThi hrudagate yebe bhAbiba anIti

<P>Abara kuru pANDabe kAhiM loDu pIrati | 35 |

<P>dhrutarASTa bolanti zuNa ho san~jay1e

[MBO-06-6]

<P>pAdAarghya deiNa ye caraNe kale dibyapUjA

<>putragoTi'' pare (jha, Ta, pha, n~a re pATha :--

<P1>gauDaku mAra boli driyodhana boilA

<P1>bAsudebaMku jhiMghAsi se aneka gALidilA |

<P1>kointAMku se ye AdihuM nindAkalA

<P1>pAde janma hoanti manuSya garbheNa |
